Bug\n\nThe JavaScript CLI (`@link-assistant/web-capture` on npm) cannot accept any URL as a positional argument. Every invocation fails with:\n\n```\nUnknown argument: https://example.com\n```\n\n## Root cause\n\nIn `js/bin/web-capture.js`, the yargs configuration uses `.strict()` (line ~228) without defining a positional parameter via `.command()`. In strict mode, yargs rejects any argument that isn't a declared option — including the URL that `main()` expects to find in `config._[0]` (line ~828).\n\n## Steps to reproduce\n\n```bash\nbun install -g @link-assistant/web-capture@latest\nweb-capture https://example.com\n# Error: Unknown argument: https://example.com\n\nweb-capture https://example.com --format markdown\n# Error: Unknown argument: https://example.com\n\nweb-capture --capture api --archive zip -- https://example.com\n# Error: Missing URL or --serve flag\n```\n\nAll three forms fail. The CLI is completely non-functional for capture mode.\n\n## Suggested fix\n\nEither:\n\n1. **Remove `.strict()`** — simplest fix, allows positional args through.\n2. **Define a positional command** — e.g., `.command('$0 [url]', ...)` so yargs knows about the URL positional.\n\nOption 2 is cleaner as it preserves strict validation for typos in option names.\n\n## Environment\n\n- `@link-assistant/web-capture` npm version: latest (reports `0.3.0` internally)\n- Node.js: v20.19.4\n- Bun: v1.2.20\n- macOS (Darwin 24.6.0)\n\n## Notes\n\n- The `--version` flag reports `0.3.0` even though the npm registry shows versions 1.1.2 → 1.7.2 — the internal version string appears out of sync with the published package version.\n- The Rust CLI (`web-capture` on crates.io, v0.3.1) works correctly with the same URLs.","closed_by":null,"reactions":{"url":"https://api.github.com/repos/link-assistant/web-capture/issues/68/reactions","total_count":0,"+1":0,"-1":0,"laugh":0,"hooray":0,"confused":0,"heart":0,"rocket":0,"eyes":0},"timeline_url":"https://api.github.com/repos/link-assistant/web-capture/issues/68/timeline","performed_via_github_app":null,"state_reason":null,"pinned_comment":null}
